## Person Spine ‚Äî global human backbone (Shared) ‚Äî Person-spine build 2026-06-25

**What:** A global `people` table (one row per human) behind every role a person plays ‚Äî lead/customer/member/invited-worker/labor-resource. The three-entity identity standard: Person √ó Organization (`businesses`) √ó Membership/role. `person_id` is an **OVERLAY, NEVER the auth principal** ‚Äî RLS stays on `user_id = auth.uid()` (documented divergence, ¬ß6.10: textbook would make the person id the principal; we don't, because RLS is proven on auth.uid() and person‚Üîauth is 1:many).
**Status:** ‚úÖ BUILDER-COMPLETE (CP1 `8eda8e3` + CP2 `c1f8be3`); migration + full-nuke wipe STAGED (David applies as postgres) ‚Äî schema-verification gate + owner-proof OWED. Close-out ledger rows #31/#32.
**Vertical:** shared | **Type:** infrastructure
**Location:** `supabase/migrations/20260625_person_spine.sql` ¬∑ `scripts/wipe-for-person-spine.sql` ¬∑ `packages/shared/src/business-logic/personUpsert.ts` ¬∑ recon `data/grower-scan/person-spine-recon.md`

**Schema (cultivar-os Supabase project ‚Äî bgobkjcopcxusjsetfob, STAGED):**
- `people` (NEW) ‚Äî `id` (person_id), `auth_user_id` (nullable UNIQUE FK‚Üíauth.users ON DELETE SET NULL ‚Äî nullable because invited-not-enrolled workers / captured customers have no auth account), `first_name`/`last_name`/`full_name`, `email`/`phone`. **NO `business_id`** (global). RLS `people_self_all` (FOR ALL, `auth_user_id = auth.uid()`) ‚Äî self-only; customer/worker persons (auth-less) created server-side with the service key. updated_at trigger + auth-less `email`/`phone` lookup indexes.
- Nullable `person_id` overlay (FK‚Üípeople ON DELETE SET NULL) added to `business_members`, `customers`, `labor_resources`, `invitations`. `customers.price_tier` (text, default `'retail'`, no CHECK ‚Äî AC-4; retail/wholesale/contractor as a TIER not an entity). Nothing forced NOT NULL.
- Migration ALTERS no existing policy/function/trigger (is_active_member, has_permission, bm_* , self-grant trigger, customers_business_owner all untouched ‚Äî overlay only).
- **Full-nuke wipe** (`scripts/wipe-for-person-spine.sql`, run once before the migration): enumerates every `business_id`-bearing table from the live catalog + discovers append-only guarded tables (`reject_*_mutation` triggers) ‚Üí **STEP B2 privileged one-time teardown** (disable guards ‚Üí `TRUNCATE ‚Ä¶ CASCADE` ‚Üí re-enable guards, one transaction so a failure auto-restores the guard) ‚Üí `DELETE FROM auth.users` ‚Üí **STEP C verifies guards back ON** + 0 rows. `audit_log` is append-only (its guard rejected the first wipe ‚Äî working as designed) and FK-cascades from businesses, so it's cleared inside the labeled teardown window, never as a quiet workaround; David owner-proves the guard is restored (manual `UPDATE audit_log` post-reset must be rejected). David chose FULL NUKE (all data expendable); the real LAWNS demo returns via Build B (per-tenant seed/reset, queued).

**Create-or-link ‚Äî ONE shared function (¬ß6.8):** `findOrCreatePerson(db, input)` resolves a human to one person row. Precedence: (1) `auth_user_id` (strongest); (2) auth-less ‚Üí email then phone (global, auth-less-only); (3) no identifier ‚Üí insert (D-9, never fabricate a key). `[TRACE:PERSON]` on every create/link/resolve. Wired (CP2) into: OwnerSignup (browser-RLS, links `business_members.person_id`), acceptInvitation (service-key, links `invitations.person_id` + activated member), customerUpsert (service-key, person-based dedup). All non-blocking (overlay; rule 6 ‚Äî never blocks an order). **Fixes the email-only-dedup bug:** a phone-only customer repeat matches the existing person by phone ‚Üí no second customer (Marcus-Webb-dupe class), with graceful fallback to legacy email-dedup if the person layer is unavailable.

## Multi-Tenant Auth System (Shared)

**What:** Full invite-based team management for any vertical. Owner invites members by email; member receives a `/join?token=...` link, creates a Supabase account, and is linked to the owner's business.  
**Status:** ‚úÖ Built ‚Äî TypeScript (merged to main 2026-06-03)  
**Vertical:** shared | **Type:** infrastructure  
**Location:** `packages/shared/src/auth/`

**Schema (cultivar-os Supabase project ‚Äî bgobkjcopcxusjsetfob):**
- `business_members` ‚Äî links `auth.uid()` to a `businesses.id`. Columns: `role`, `permissions` (text[]), `active`, `pin_hash` (added 2026-06-03). RLS: owner full access, member reads own row.
- `invitations` ‚Äî pending invite tokens. 7-day expiry. `used` flag prevents replay. RLS: owner full access.
- `member_devices` ‚Äî optional device tracking (denormalized `business_id` for RLS without join).
- **Migration pending (David):** `supabase/migrations/20260603_business_members_add_pin_hash.sql` adds `pin_hash` to business_members in bgobkjcopcxusjsetfob.

**Shared TypeScript modules:**
- `auth/types.ts` ‚Äî `Member`, `Invitation`, `Role`, `VerticalAdapter`, `AcceptInviteResult`, `InvitePreview`
- `auth/members.ts` ‚Äî `getMembersByBusiness`, `updateMemberRole`, `removeMember`, `checkPermission(permissions[], name)`
- `auth/invitations.ts` ‚Äî `createInvitation`, `revokeInvitation`, `getPendingInvitations`, `expireInvitations`
- `auth/acceptInvitation.ts` ‚Äî `previewInvitation`, `acceptInvitation` (service-key server functions)
- `auth/AcceptInvite.tsx` ‚Äî React accept-invite page component (inline styles, TRACE green)
- `auth/OwnerSignup.tsx` ‚Äî Multi-step signup with PIN: Owner Info ‚Üí PIN Setup ‚Üí Biometric (optional) ‚Üí vertical steps. Config-driven. Added 2026-06-03. Updated 2026-06-04: `backgroundColor`, `cardColor`, `examples` fields added to config (removes hardcoded Cultivar sage/white; enables Ignition dark theme).
- `auth/permissions.ts` ‚Äî Pure permission check helpers (added 2026-06-10, THUNDER ¬∑ BUILD 2):
  - `can(session, permId)` ‚Äî null-safe check for a permission string in session.permissions[]
  - `hasRole(session, roleName)` ‚Äî null-safe session.role equality check
  - `canAccessModule(allowed, moduleKey)` ‚Äî checks the Ignition-specific `allowed[]` shortlist (derived from view_* permissions by auth.ts authenticate())
  - `expandRoles(policy, roleNames)` ‚Äî expands role-badge strings ‚Üí flat union of permission strings; replaces the DataBridge.getSystemRoles() + flatMap pattern in CoreApp.jsx
  - `deriveAllowed(permissions)` ‚Äî strips 'view_' prefix; matches the derivation in auth.ts and CoreApp.jsx JoinFlow
  - `PermissionPolicy` interface ‚Äî vertical passes `{ roles: Record<string, string[]> }` as config data (AC-1: role names are string values, not TypeScript identifiers)
  - These are drop-in replacements for inline checks; callers NOT migrated yet (Ignition migration deferred to post-pilot_all fix, TD#28)
- `discovery/DiscoveryGlimpse.tsx` ‚Äî Client-only React component (VerticalStep). Loads website from businesses table, fires /api/discovery/ingest, renders REAL profile findings only. Import directly (not from barrel) to avoid bundling server-side SDK deps. Added 2026-06-04. **FAIL-LOUD + persistence 2026-06-25 (`c8094e1`, FIX 1):** it previously collapsed no-profile/API-error/network-failure into `phase='done'` and rendered canned `NURSERY_SEED_INSIGHTS` as "Strengths" under "Here's what we found" (canned copy as findings; the `'error'` Phase had no render branch). Now: a real returned profile is the only path to `done`; failures land on a new honest `error` phase (retry / manual-entry / skip); analyzing-phase teasers reframed "What we look for"; **businessId is now passed in the POST body so `ingest.ts:171 seedServiceOfferings` persists** (was omitted ‚Üí analysis ran, nothing saved). `[TRACE:DISCOVERY]` on run/success/failure. BUILDER-COMPLETE; owner-proof owed.
- `auth/index.ts` ‚Äî barrel export
- `supabase/auth.ts` ‚Äî `hashPin()`, `authenticate()` (queries shop_members, returns AuthSession with role/permissions/allowed), `authenticateMember()` (queries business_members, returns MemberSession), `getMemberSession()`, `clearMemberSession()`, `getTrialStatus()`.

**Cultivar OS integration:**
- `api/members/preview-invite.ts` / `accept-invite.ts` ‚Äî Vercel handlers (consolidated into `/api/members/invite` as GET+POST)
- `src/pages/Settings.tsx` TeamSection ‚Äî invite form, member list, pending invitations, copy-link UI
- `src/router.tsx` ‚Äî public `/join` route ‚Üí `AcceptInvite` component
- `src/auth/roles.ts` ‚Äî OWNER / MANAGER / STAFF role definitions with permission arrays

**Permission model ‚Äî Cultivar OS (business_members table):**
- `null` permissions = owner (full access implied). `string[]` = member's explicit DB-stored permissions.
- Gate expression: `const canX = isOwner || (userPermissions ?? []).includes('permission_key')`
- MANAGER excludes `manage_settings` by design ‚Äî cannot reach Settings page

**Permission model ‚Äî Ignition OS (shop_members table, PILOT phase):**
- Roles: TECH / SERVICE / ADMIN (canonical, from shop_members); SUB_ROLES: SR_TECH/BAY_TECH/APPRENTICE (TECH), ADVISOR/CASHIER (SERVICE)
- `allowed[]` = permissions filtered to view_* ‚Üí strip prefix. Gate: `session.allowed.includes('flux')` etc.
- Role presets defined in `IgnitionAdmin.jsx:ROLE_PRESETS` (TECH/SERVICE/ADMIN ‚Üí capability string arrays)
- `DataBridge.getSystemRoles()` uses OLD role-badge format (ADMIN/TECH/CUSTOMER); JoinFlow members use NEW capability-string format ‚Äî these two formats are incompatible in the `userCapabilities` expansion path
- ‚öÝÔ∏è All enforcement is CLIENT-SIDE ONLY ‚Äî see Tech Debt #28 (pilot_all wide-open RLS)

**Test coverage:** `scripts/test-member-login.mjs` ‚Äî 8 sections, 29 assertions against live DB. Verified: owner path, member path, MANAGER permission exclusions, LAWNS-specific invite flow.

## BusinessProvider (Shared Context)

**What:** React context that resolves the logged-in user's business and exposes it across the app. Two-path resolution: owner fast-path, member fallback.  
**Status:** ‚úÖ Built ‚Äî TypeScript  
**Vertical:** shared | **Type:** infrastructure  
**Location:** `packages/shared/src/context/BusinessProvider.tsx`  
**Exports:** `BusinessProvider`, `useBusinessContext`, `Business`, `BusinessContextValue` (from `packages/shared/src/context/index.ts`)

**Resolution logic:**
1. Owner path (fast): `businesses WHERE owner_id = auth.uid() AND business_type = $type`
2. Member fallback (if owner returns null): `business_members WHERE user_id = auth.uid() AND active = true` with `businesses(*)` PostgREST join, filtered post-fetch to `business_type === businessType`

**Context values:**
- `business: Business | null` ‚Äî full businesses row
- `businessId: string | null`
- `businessError: string | null` ‚Äî `'no_business'` when both paths genuinely return zero rows; `'read_error'` when a resolution SELECT ERRORED (data=null, rows may exist). Distinct since 2026-06-24 (`97118ef`): the owner + member SELECTs capture `{ error }` and emit `[TRACE:BUSINESS] owner/member path ERROR {code,message,details,hint}`, so an errored read no longer masquerades as `no_business`. Query shape + RLS unchanged.
- `loading: boolean` ‚Äî stays `true` across the **bounded write-then-read retry** (2026-06-24 `56c7f81`): a fresh signup runs the resolution read ~1ms before the create write is visible (HAR-confirmed ‚Äî every read 200, just empty). The owner+member resolution (`attemptResolution()`) re-runs up to `RESOLVE_MAX_ATTEMPTS=3` times, `~500ms` apart (~1s total), stopping early on first non-empty result or a real query error; `no_business` is set only after retries exhaust (SETTLED). Emits `[TRACE:BUSINESS] resolution retry {attempt, reason:'empty_with_session'}`. Consumers (Dashboard) redirect to `/onboarding` ONLY when settled (`loading===false`), so the first transient empty read no longer bounce-loops onboarding.
- `reload: () => void`
- `userPermissions: string[] | null` ‚Äî null = owner, string[] = member's DB-stored permissions
- `isOwner: boolean`

**Consumed by:** `packages/cultivar-os/src/App.tsx` (`<BusinessProvider businessType="nursery">`), all Cultivar pages via `useBusinessContext()`.

**Security note (fixed 2026-06-04, commit 8792c71):** Member path filters by `business_type` after fetching ‚Äî `memberBiz?.business_type === businessType` must match before the member resolution is accepted. This prevents cross-vertical data exposure (audit finding #13). If a user is a member of multiple businesses in the same vertical, `.single()` will fail ‚Äî acceptable for v1.

---

## QBO Customer Identity Resolution ‚Äî the three-way rule (D-47) ‚Äî added 2026-07-16

**What:** How a TRACE customer resolves to a QuickBooks customer on the invoice push. Replaces an
email-only match that cross-billed **nine real invoices to the wrong person over two months**.
**Status:** üü° BUILDER-COMPLETE ‚Äî owner-proof owed (ledger #130) | **Vertical:** shared + cultivar | **Type:** correctness / integration
**Location:** `packages/shared/src/quickbooks/customerIdentity.ts` (the ONE decision fn ‚Äî pure, 22 tests) ¬∑
`packages/shared/src/utils/personName.ts` (person-name canonical key) ¬∑
`packages/cultivar-os/api/qbo/invoice/cultivar.ts` (the IO + stored-link verification)

**The rule ‚Äî two independent fields must CONCUR before TRACE binds an identity:**

| email match | name match | action |
|---|---|---|
| yes | yes | **LINK** |
| no | no | **CREATE** |
| **YES** | **NO** | **CREATE** ‚Üê the Terrence case; never link |
| no | YES | **SURFACE** (409, owner resolves) |

**Root asymmetry (the lesson):** QBO enforces `DisplayName` **UNIQUE**; QBO does **NOT** enforce
unique email (families and offices share one). TRACE matched on the one field QBO permits to
collide and ignored the one it guarantees. ‚Üí **Match on the field the external system guarantees
unique.** ‚Üí ‚úÖ **STD-019** (ACTIVATED 2026-07-16, STANDARDS.md v2.4) ‚Äî generalizes to any external
identity binding (Stripe, supplier catalogs), not just QBO.

**Also:** a stored `qb_customer_id` is a **CACHE, not a fact** ‚Äî verified against the live QBO
record before billing (name drift ‚Üí refuse + flag; this is the check that would have caught the bug
on invoice #1 instead of #9). Collision guard (two TRACE customers may never share one
`qb_customer_id`, business_id-scoped). QBO 6240 duplicate-DisplayName **surfaces**; the silent
email-as-DisplayName junk-record fallback is **retired**. Closes tech-debt #53.

**No readback exists** (recon 2026-07-16): nothing imports QBO customers into `customers`, so the
matcher is load-bearing ‚Äî without it any party predating TRACE 6240s on every push. The three
readback-looking artifacts (`pullQBOCustomers`, `ExternalBridge.qbo.pullCustomers`,
`QuickBooksConnector.jsx`) are dead Railway-era code hitting a deleted endpoint.

**‚öÝÔ∏è Reuse note:** does **NOT** use the #61 `nameTokenSet` ‚Äî that key splits on apostrophes
(`O'Brien`‚Üí`{brien}` ‚âÝ `OBrien`‚Üí`{obrien}`) because it drops 1-char tokens for the botanical hybrid
`x`. `personName.ts` elides apostrophes and reuses `tokenSetsEqual`. **The same blind spot is a
LATENT bug in the plant resolver** (slug `baileys-red-twig-dogwood` won't match `Bailey's Red Twig
Dogwood`) ‚Äî flagged, not fixed.

**Decision:** `docs/decisions/2026-07-16-qbo-customer-identity-resolution-D47.md`

## QB Token Refresh

**What:** Proactive QuickBooks token refresh. Checks expiry before any invoice call. Refreshes if missing or within 10 min of expiry. Sets `qb_needs_reconnect=true` and returns null if refresh token is dead.  
**Status:** ‚úÖ Built ‚Äî TypeScript  
**Vertical:** shared | **Type:** infrastructure  
**Location:** `packages/shared/src/quickbooks/refresh.ts`  
**Used by:** `packages/cultivar-os/api/qbo/invoice/cultivar.ts`

**‚öÝÔ∏è QB integration scope: receivables only (Audit 6, 2026-06-06).** The current QB integration (`api/qbo/`) covers invoices (money IN) and customer lookup/create. Payables (money OUT ‚Äî expense write, Attachable image archive, Chart of Accounts query, Purchase/Bill write) are confirmed API-capable but NOT yet wired in TRACE code. Payables wire-up = Receipt Keeper v2 scope. See `docs/audits/2026-06-06-audits-5-6-quickbooks.md` ¬ß6b.

**‚úÖ RESOLVED 2026-06-08 ‚Äî proactive expiry surfacing live.** `qbo/status.ts` now checks `accounting_token_expires_at` on every dashboard load; attempts silent `refreshQBToken()` if expired; returns `needsReconnect: true` if refresh fails. `Dashboard.tsx` derives the banner immediately from `accounting_token_expires_at` client-side and applies the authoritative server result from `checkQbStatus()`. A dead/expired connection now announces itself on page load ‚Äî no mid-use 401 required. STD-007 added as the class-of-bug record.

**‚úÖ RESOLVED 2026-06-19 ‚Äî QB routes 500 root-caused + fixed (commit `14a9a82`, tech-debt #34).** Both `/api/qbo/auth-url` and `/api/qbo/status` returned `FUNCTION_INVOCATION_FAILED`. Root cause: `packages/cultivar-os/api/qbo/router.ts:15` imported `refreshQBToken` from `../../../../shared/...` (FOUR `../` ‚Üí nonexistent `<repo-root>/shared/`); router.ts sits at `api/qbo/` so the correct depth is THREE `../` (now `../../../shared/src/quickbooks/refresh` ‚Äî confirmed `router.ts:15`). The unresolved import crashed the function at module load ‚Üí 500 on every qbo route regardless of token state. Proven via esbuild (old path fails resolution, new bundles clean). Connect flow now reaches the auth-url link instead of 500.

## Social Media Module (shared + Cultivar OS surface)

**What:** Period-based AI social post generator. Aggregates the week's sales into platform-specific captions. Owner edits, copies to clipboard, posts manually.  
**Status:** ‚úÖ Generator moved to shared 2026-06-08 ‚Äî business_type-parameterized, Sonnet via gateway. Table de-nouned (AC-1). Edit/save widget live.  
**Vertical:** shared (generator) + cultivar (surface) | **Type:** tile  

**Backend:**
- `packages/shared/src/social/generate.ts` ‚Äî `generateSocialDrafts()` ‚Äî business_type-parameterized, Sonnet via AI gateway. `BUSINESS_DESCRIPTORS` map: variation is data, not code. `[TRACE:socialdraft]` behind `SOCIALDRAFT_DEBUG`.
- `packages/cultivar-os/api/social/generate-posts.ts` ‚Äî thin Vercel handler: reads context (orders, plants, config) ‚Üí calls shared generator ‚Üí inserts to `social_drafts` with `subject_type='inventory'`, `subject_id=null`.
- `packages/cultivar-os/api/social/enable.ts` ‚Äî upserts `business_modules` with `{ advert_channels: AdvertChannel[], cadence }`. No blotato_account_id. `advert_channels` is the single source of truth for all channel config (social + SMS).

**social_drafts table (de-nouned 2026-06-08):**
- Columns: `id, business_id, platform, original_text, edited_text, status, subject_type, subject_id, cadence, period_start, period_end, copied_at, post_type, created_at`
- `original_text`: immutable AI proposal. `edited_text`: what owner saved (null until edited).
- `subject_type`/`subject_id`: AC-1 compliant subject ref (value, not column name). Cultivar writes `subject_type='inventory'`, `subject_id=null` for period aggregates.
- Status lifecycle: `draft ‚Üí edited ‚Üí approved ‚Üí copied` (+ `copied_at` timestamp).
- **No** `content`, `order_id`, `plant_id` (all retired 2026-06-08).
- **`social_drafts_platform_check` (2026-06-09):** CHECK constraint now migration-controlled. Hand-applied pre-migration-era; original allowed list was `(instagram, facebook, tiktok, twitter)`. Extended to include `'sms'` by `supabase/migrations/20260609_social_drafts_platform_check.sql`. ‚öÝÔ∏è Migration pending David apply + verify. Without this: SMS-enabled generation runs write zero rows (atomic batch rolls back when sms row violates constraint).

**Dashboard edit/save widget:**
- Generate button ‚Üí calls `/api/social/generate-posts` ‚Üí inserts drafts ‚Üí `loadSocialDrafts()` reloads.
- Draft card: editable textarea (original_text); on blur ‚Üí `handleSaveEdit()` ‚Üí writes `edited_text + status='edited'`.
- [Copy] button ‚Üí copies to clipboard + `status='copied' + copied_at` ‚Üí removes from queue.
- [Download image] ‚Äî stub, disabled (seam declared below).
- [Open platform] ‚Äî links to platform URL.
- Edited drafts show green border + "‚úì Edited" chip.

**Voice-delta captured (seam declared):**  
`original_text` vs `edited_text` = the training delta, accumulating now, no consumer yet.  
**remaining:** voice-learning BI ‚Äî query original vs edited pairs to detect voice patterns. Horizon: v2/later. NOT a defect ‚Äî data is flowing cleanly; the analysis surface is the unfilled seam.

**Aggregation/cadence generator (seam declared):**  
`cadence` is stored per module config; `period_start`/`period_end` captured per draft. The generator that reads `config.cadence` and auto-triggers a new generation window (preventing per-purchase overwhelm) is the next step.  
**remaining:** cadence-triggered generation ‚Äî scheduler that fires generate-posts on cadence rhythm. Horizon: Social Rhythm (next social session). NOT a defect ‚Äî the data model is ready; the trigger is the unfilled seam.

**advert_channels config (2026-06-08):**
`business_modules.config.advert_channels: [{type:'social'|'sms', name:string, enabled:boolean}]` ‚Äî flat typed list. `generate-posts.ts` reads this and generates ONLY for enabled channels. SMS is a separate entry (`type:'sms'`, always one post, no image prompt). LEXICON RULE: "platform" is reserved for the top-level TRACE substrate; "channel"/"advert_channel" is used inside the product.

**Not built:** image generation. Direct social publishing ‚Äî Blotato removed 2026-06-08 (misrepresented capability).

**Hidden seams declared (inert, demand-gated, priced ‚Äî see `api/campaigns.ts` preamble):**
- `auto-publish seam` ‚Äî wire a vetted publisher adapter at activation. No refactor needed. Gate: demand + pricing.
- `sms-auto-send seam` ‚Äî TCPA/10DLC/opt-out compliance is real work at activation; adopt provider model. Gate: demand + pricing + provider selection.

## QR Checkout Flow (Cultivar OS)

**What:** Complete scan-to-invoice flow. QR scan ‚Üí plant profile ‚Üí add-ons ‚Üí customer capture ‚Üí cart review ‚Üí order submit ‚Üí QB invoice ‚Üí email confirmation. **Now MULTI-ITEM** (2026-07-08): scan many items into ONE order, services attach by rule, owner adjusts before submit.  
**Order roster + CRUD (2026-07-08, ledger #100 ‚Äî BUILDER-COMPLETE, owner-proof owed):** the `/orders` roster names every order by the **D-34 dual anchor** (specimen `cultivar_plants` wins, else stock-line `business_inventory.name`) ‚Äî closes the "Unknown plant" gap on scan/stock-line orders (`lib/orderItemName.ts`, reused roster + drill-in). NEW `/orders/:id` drill-in (`pages/OrderDetail.tsx`) shows ALL line items + ALL services (`order_service_selections`, previously written-but-never-shown) + customer + delivery date + status + totals. **Owner/manager CRUD** (`api/orders/submit.ts` action=update|delete|status, token-gated: owner by `owner_id` OR `manage_orders` perm; staff READ-ONLY, server-enforced): edit line qty + delivery date, remove lines, change status (`pending‚Üíconfirmed‚Üífulfilled‚Üícancelled`, `lib/orderStatus.ts`), delete ‚Äî each SERVER-RECOMPUTED (re-read `sell_price`, re-net services) with inventory RE-RESERVED (release old/reserve new) / RELEASED on delete. QB-invoice staleness surfaced on edit (R-QBSTALE). NEW shared server-gate `packages/shared/src/auth/callerPermission.ts` (`callerHoldsPermission` moved from ingest.ts + `callerIsBusinessOwner`). ZERO schema, ZERO new api-fn (12/12). Open: R-QBSTALE, R-STATUS. **Follow-up (2026-07-08):** the drill-in showed "PLANTS (0)" while the subtotal included plant cost ‚Äî a PostgREST nested-embed drop (order_items embed under the `.maybeSingle()` orders query returned `[]` while the sibling services embed populated). FIXED: `order_items` fetched in its OWN top-level query (`ITEM_COLS`), anchor-agnostic, names via the same `orderItemName.ts` resolver; `[TRACE:ROSTER]` now logs line count + anchors + a subtotal reconciliation. Completes the drill-in. **Fix (2026-07-15, ledger #129, migration GATED):** the status-change write (`action=status`) was **500-ing** on `confirmed`/`fulfilled` ‚Äî the live `orders.status` carried a pre-D-37 CHECK `CHECK (status = ANY (ARRAY['pending','invoiced','paid','cancelled']))` (a payment lifecycle) that rejected the code's fulfillment vocabulary; undetected because every order sat at `pending`. ONE gated migration `20260715_orders_status_drop_check.sql` DROPs the constraint (AC-1/STD-011/D-37 ‚Äî `ORDER_STATUSES` in code is the canonical guard; handleStatus already validates ‚Üí clean 400 on a bad value). NO app-code change. **R-STATUS blocking defect CLOSED ‚Äî ‚úÖ OWNER-PROVEN 2026-07-15** (David, live: migration applied + catalog-verified A‚ÄìC; Confirmed/Fulfilled/Cancelled all persist with no 500; Cancelled restores stock per D-42; bad value still returns clean 400). Sibling `orders_transport_method_check` flagged as the same class (tech-debt #52).  
**SERVICE PRICE OVERRIDE IS A DISCOUNT ‚Äî the QBO `6070` fix (2026-07-16, D-48 proposed, **committed + PUSHED `5f16c42`**, BUILDER-COMPLETE, owner-proof owed; ledger #131; ZERO migration, ZERO api-fn 12/12):** üü° **THE SCAR (live, CLV-20260716-1156):** the owner overrode Placement Service $1575‚Üí$1000 and the line was written `retailUnit 225 ¬∑ qty 7 ¬∑ retailTotal 1575 ¬∑ discountAmt 0 ¬∑ netTotal 1000` ‚Äî **the line CONTRADICTED ITSELF** (1575 ‚àí 0 ‚âÝ 1000). **QuickBooks was the FIRST thing anywhere downstream that multiplied rate √ó qty** and REJECTED the invoice: `6070 "Amount is not equal to UnitPrice * Qty. Supplied value:1,000"` (2 pushes, 16:57 + 17:19; the invoice does not exist in QBO). Silent because every TRACE surface rendered $1000 and reconciled cleanly ($2020 / 7.6% $153.52 / $2173.52 ‚Äî all correct): **no TRACE surface checks that a LINE is internally consistent** ‚Äî every check we had looked at *aggregates ACROSS* lines, and the defect lived *WITHIN* one. **ROOT:** D-43 SPECCED the invariant `retail_total ‚àí discount_amt === net_total` and verified it in a MIGRATION ‚Äî which passed **only because no override existed yet**; nothing enforced it where lines are BORN. **An invariant that is only verified in a migration is not enforced.** **BUILT (David's ruling ‚Äî an override IS a discount; supersedes D-39's "leakage ‚âÝ discount" service branch):** (1) `computeOrderPricing`'s service branch PRESERVES the retail baseline and puts the concession in `discountAmt` 575 / `discountPct` 36.51 (= `round2(discountAmt/retailTotal √ó 100)`, convention stated) ‚Äî the baseline is what makes the giveaway visible AND what lets QBO multiply and agree; (2) the invariant is **ENFORCED AT COMPUTE TIME and THROWS** (half-cent tolerance for float dust) ‚Äî unfireable by construction, it guards the next branch that forgets; (3) an **UPWARD override is a NEGATIVE discount (surcharge) ‚Äî ALLOWED** (refusing would REGRESS an ability the owner has today; stays consistent `1575 ‚àí (‚àí425) = 2000`; pushes a positive "price adjusted" line; pct honest-negative, never rendered as "% off"); (4) **`discountTotal` restricted to GOODS-only + NEW `serviceAdjustmentTotal`** ‚Äî the structural trap: `discountTotal`'s contract already SAID "goods only" but summed EVERY line, getting away with it *only because services were hardcoded to 0*; the $575 would have leaked into the "<tier> ‚Äî N% off" line rendered against `goodsRetailSubtotal` (STD-011 ‚Äî a tier discount and an owner concession are two DIFFERENT facts: different authority, label, audit trail); (5) **reason REQUIRED** (STD-013, reusing D-40's exemption shape) at UI (`Reason *` + surfaced error, no silent no-op) **and** server (`applyOverride` refuses + logs + charges the BASELINE ‚Äî refusal charges MORE, the money-safe direction) **and** spine (so the gates agree by construction) ‚Äî **NO MIGRATION: `override_reason` already existed on `order_service_selections` AND `order_items` (20260708:27,36), applied, and submit already WROTE it; it was simply never REQUIRED**; (6) **QBO** pushes the service at RETAIL (`225 √ó 7 = 1575` ‚Äî internally consistent, accepted) + the 575 on the SAME negative-Amount mechanism as the tier discount via ONE extracted **`discountLine()`** helper (STD-011 ‚Äî no forked second discount path), GATED so a normal order pushes byte-identical (zero regression), plus a NEW **reconcile check** that refuses to push when the lines don't sum to the order total (so a discount line can never double-count against an already-netted line); (7) **Confirmation (D-9)** ‚Äî the type was `'success' | 'pending'`, so **there was no failed state to render**: a hard 400 rendered *"‚è± Invoice will sync shortly ‚Äî Connect QuickBooks from the owner dashboard"*, wrong twice (QBO WAS connected, having minted customer 84 seconds earlier; and nothing would ever sync). Now THREE honest states `success | not_connected` (503 only) `| failed` (reason surfaced), scoped by `ownerView` ‚Äî the owner gets the error + action, the customer a true neutral state with no internals and **no owner instruction** (which the old copy handed to customers on the public QR path). **‚öÝÔ∏è CAUGHT DURING THE BUILD:** `CartReview` fed `overrideTotal` WITHOUT `overrideReason` ‚Üí Review would have shown $1575 while submit charged $1000 ‚Äî the exact STD-012 divergence, re-created by the fix for a different bug; fixed same pass. **RECORDED:** `tierPricing.test.ts` test 16 asserted `discountAmt === 0` ‚Äî **the defect was TESTED IN and blessed**; the suite asked whether the override replaced the charge (it did), never whether the line still added up (it didn't). Rewritten to assert the invariant, with that history in the file. **This fix MOVES NO MONEY** ($2173.52 to the penny). `[TRACE:PRICE]`/`[TRACE:LEAKAGE]`/`[TRACE:QBO]` ON (each line logs `invariantOk`). `npm run verify` exit 0 zero net-new; **138/138** tier-pricing tests (was 84; +54, RED-first per STD-002). **Flagged (NOT built):** `apply_discount` is DECLARED but not the gate (rides `manage_orders` + the server token gate ‚Äî documented-with-reason); goods overrides don't exist yet (service-only by contract ‚Üí **no stacking question today**), but when a plant-line override is built it WILL be one (the tier discount already occupies goods' `discountAmt`) ‚Äî David decides then. Home: `docs/decisions/2026-07-16-service-price-override-is-a-discount-D48.md`.
**INVENTORY DECREMENT-ON-PAID ‚Äî the missing per-unit stock depletion (2026-07-13, D-42 proposed, BUILDER-COMPLETE, migration gated, owner-proof owed; ledger #120):** üü° RECON verdict: a qty decrement NEVER existed ‚Äî the order path only flipped a whole lot's `status` to `'reserved'` on ANY sale (submit.ts ¬ß11), which under D-34 (lot=SKU, qty=count) wrongly reserved all 45 of a 45-lot when 1 sold + hid the lot from the status-filtered dashboard `available_count` (the vanishing that *looked* like depletion). **MODEL (David, Amazon standard):** decrement `qty` PER-UNIT at ORDER-PAID/CONFIRMED (checkout complete + invoice generated ‚Äî the ¬ß11 point), NOT at delivery (delivery is a later event that does NOT touch qty). **BUILT:** (1) ONE atomic RPC **`adjust_inventory_qty(p_lot_id, p_business_id, p_delta)`** ‚Äî a single guarded UPDATE (`qty + delta >= 0` = the oversell guard), concurrency-safe (NO JS read-modify-write, so two concurrent orders on one lot can't lose a unit), status DERIVES from the new qty (qty>0‚Üí'available', qty<=0‚Üí'depleted' ‚Äî the existing datasheet vocabulary; a manual 'damaged'/'returned' is preserved), `SECURITY DEFINER`/`search_path=''`, `service_role`-only EXECUTE (the RPC trusts its business_id arg ‚Üí server-only, never `authenticated`). (2) ¬ß11 decrements `‚àíquantity` targeting the RECONCILED anchor `rl.stockLineId ?? rl.plant.inventory_id` (was `plant.inventory_id`-only ‚Üí could silently no-op on a stock-line line). (3) whole order lifecycle coherent through the SAME signed-delta RPC (STD-011/STD-012): **edit** `¬±(oldQty‚àínewQty)` per lot, **delete/cancel** restore `+n` (guarded vs double-restore on an already-cancelled order). (4) OVERSELL surfaced never silent (D-9): a pre-flight `INSUFFICIENT_STOCK` 400 refuses the whole order before any write + the ¬ß11 RPC guard covers the concurrent-depletion race ‚Äî qty never driven negative. (5) `reorder_point int` stub column (nullable, additive) for the NEXT build (reorder threshold). Old `setLotStatus` whole-lot-flip helper removed. **ONE additive gated migration `20260713_inventory_decrement_and_reorder.sql`** (column + RPC ‚Äî David applies as postgres). **ZERO new api-fn** (the RPC is a Postgres function, NOT a Vercel fn ‚Äî 12/12 held). `[TRACE:INVENTORY]` ON. `npm run verify` exit 0 zero net-new. **UNBLOCKS reconciliation** (counted vs expected = last count ‚àí sold) ‚Äî was gated on real depletion. Home: `docs/decisions/2026-07-13-inventory-decrement-on-paid-D42.md`. Supersedes the whole-lot 'reserved' reservation model.

**Status:** ‚úÖ Built and live ‚Äî end-to-end  
**Vertical:** cultivar | **Type:** tile  
**Route (single-item):** `/plant/:sku` ‚Üí `/plant/:sku/addons` ‚Üí `/checkout/customer` ‚Üí `/checkout/review` ‚Üí `/checkout/confirm`
**Route (multi-item):** `/checkout/scan` (scan-loop) ‚Üí `/checkout/addons` ‚Üí `/checkout/customer` ‚Üí `/checkout/review` ‚Üí `/checkout/confirm`

Wording-only ‚Äî no behavior change; checkout already takes no money and CartReview offers email-invoice vs pay-at-office.

**CHECKOUT FIX-PASS ‚Äî 4 owner-prove-surfaced fixes (2026-07-08, BUILDER-COMPLETE, owner-proof owed; story MAPS-TO 2.1):** üü° The #97/#98 owner-prove surfaced four gaps (as-built recon ¬ß1b/¬ß4/¬ß7). **NO new `api/` file** (rides `submit.ts`, 12/12 held); ONE gated migration for FIX 4. **FIX 1 (search lookup):** NEW shared `searchStockLines(supabase, businessId, term, {columns,limit})` in `stockLineResolver.ts` ‚Äî partial `sku`/`name` substring OR name token-subset, business_id-scoped, capped/sorted. `QrScanner` gained an optional `onLookup` prop ‚Üí the ScanOrder manual "Look up"‚Üí"Search" field now SEARCHES (partial "vitex"/"shoal"/"SCV" ‚Üí matching lot(s)); **SELL_PRICE ‚Äî the cart now charges the stock line's sell_price, not unit_cost (2026-07-07, D-35, spec item 1 ‚Äî BUILDER-COMPLETE, M1 GATED, owner-proof owed):** üü° stored `business_inventory.sell_price numeric(10,2)` (M1 migration `20260707_business_inventory_sell_price.sql`, nullable, DISTINCT from unit_cost ‚Äî **GATED, David applies**). Set inline on the `/inventory` datasheet (`BusinessInventory.tsx` sell_price AmountCell). Every cart price-read repointed `unit_cost ‚Üí sell_price`: `usePlant.ts` join, `PlantProfile.tsx`, `AddOns.tsx`, `CartReview.tsx`, `useSubmitOrder.ts`, and the server-authoritative charge in `api/orders/submit.ts` (order_items.unit_price + subtotal off sell_price; tamper-defense kept). **$0/null REFUSED (Surface Honesty, D-9):** `submit.ts` returns 400 `NO_SELL_PRICE` (no $0 order written) + CartReview shows a banner and disables the pay buttons. **`price_tier` at checkout = APPLIED (AC-4 hold CLOSED 2026-07-09):** tier‚Üídiscount math DEFINED = percent-off-baseline, owner-set per tier, default 0% (D-35 addendum `docs/decisions/2026-07-09-tier-pricing-mechanism.md`). `submit.ts` reads `price_tier`(customer) + `pricingTiers`(business config) SERVER-SIDE and applies the shared `applyTierDiscount` per line (tamper-defended; retail/unknown/0% ‚Üí unchanged). % set in Settings Cost-to-Produce Block 5; tier tagged on the `/customers` roster. No new Vercel function (edits existing submit.ts). `[TRACE:PRICE]` ON.

AC-1 (names only `business_inventory`), AC-3 (business_id-scoped). ## OwnerSignup (Shared)

**What:** Multi-step shared owner signup component with PIN gesture layer. Step 1: Owner Info (business name, owner name, email, password, phone, address, website). Step 2: PIN setup. Step 3: Biometric registration (optional, skippable). Optional vertical steps array.  
**Status:** ‚úÖ Built 2026-06-03 ‚Äî shared, consumed by both Cultivar and Ignition  
**Vertical:** shared | **Type:** infrastructure  
**Location:** `packages/shared/src/auth/OwnerSignup.tsx`

**Config-driven:** Each vertical provides an `OwnerSignupConfig` specifying `memberTable`, `memberFKColumn`, `ownerRole`, `ownerPermissions`, `pinLength`, `backgroundColor`, `cardColor`, `examples` (per-vertical placeholder text), `verticalSteps` (optional post-biometric steps), and an `onSuccess` callback. The vertical's `onSuccess` handles post-signup vertical-specific setup (e.g., Ignition creates the matching `shops` row and seeds DataBridge; Cultivar navigates to /onboarding).

**PIN hash:** SHA-256 of `{businessId}:{pin}` ‚Äî consistent with `hashPin()` in `packages/shared/src/supabase/auth.ts`.

**Retry-aware:** If "User already registered" ‚Üí attempts signIn ‚Üí if no businesses row ‚Üí continues business creation. Handles orphaned auth users from partial prior signups.

**Person-name (full_name) layer ‚Äî 2026-06-24 (`73498ca`):** the LOCKED identity model is implemented at the name write/seed layer. PERSON NAME source of truth = `auth.user_metadata.full_name`; `business_members.name` = invite-bootstrap / display-fallback only; display precedence everywhere = `full_name ‚Üí member.name ‚Üí email`. `signUp` now seeds `options.data.full_name` from the typed ownerName (was stranded ‚Äî wrote only to the member row). Same `full_name` seed mirrored in the legacy `configureAuth.tsx` and `OnboardingWizard.tsx` signup paths. `acceptInvitation.ts` seeds `user_metadata.full_name` for new invitees and bridges an existing user who has no `full_name` yet (never overwrites a real name). `Profile.tsx` member self-edit writes `auth.updateUser({full_name})` first (unified with the owner path; member.name kept in sync as fallback; authority boundary held ‚Äî name/phone/email only, never role/permissions). `BusinessProvider` member display precedence corrected to `authName ?? memberName ?? email`. NO schema/RLS/owner_id changes. **BUILDER-COMPLETE; owner-proof owed** (new owner signup ‚Üí header shows name not email; member name self-edit persists/displays; invite accept carries name).

**Onboarding bounce-loop fixes ‚Äî 2026-06-24 (`97118ef`):** two independent swallow fixes in `OnboardingWizard.finalize()` + a gated migration. (1) **finalize now checks the `nursery_profiles` upsert `{ error }`** ‚Äî on error it emits `[TRACE:BUSINESS] onboarding finalize: nursery_profiles upsert ERROR` and sets `finalizeError` (blocking the false "is live"/DONE screen) instead of advancing over a failed write. (2) **`20260624_nursery_profiles_business_id_unique.sql`** (gated, NOT applied) adds `UNIQUE (business_id)` so the `onConflict:'business_id'` upsert stops raising 42P10 ‚Üí 400 (a `nursery_profiles` row is 1:1 with a business). Pre-existing bugs, NOT caused by `73498ca`. **BUILDER-COMPLETE; owner-proof owed** (apply the migration as postgres + catalog-verify the UNIQUE; finalize over a failed write shows an error, not "is live"). See also the `BusinessProvider` `read_error` distinction above (the masked dashboard-read error that caused the bounce).

**Phone-field consolidation ‚Äî 2026-06-24 (`b7ed4b7`):** phone recon mapped 3 inputs ‚Üí 2 real destinations + 1 dead field + 1 latent duplicate-create hazard; this consolidates without merging the two genuine destinations (business phone vs personal phone). (1) **Dead onboarding phone removed** ‚Äî the `OnboardingWizard` "Your Nursery" Phone field only wrote inside `finalize()`'s skipped `if(!businessId)` legacy branch, so the typed value was dropped on every normal signup; removed end-to-end. (2) **Duplicate-create guard** ‚Äî that legacy `businesses` INSERT now re-resolves the user's business at finalize before inserting (settled re-read), so the write-then-read race can no longer create a SECOND `businesses` row; genuinely business-less manual-nav still creates (branch GUARDED not removed). (3) **Owner-profile phone** ‚Äî `Profile.tsx` owner branch gains an editable Phone row wired to the EXISTING `saveMemberField('phone')` writer (`business_members.phone`, own row). Owners DO have a member row (OwnerSignup creates it; `BusinessProvider:341` dedupes it out of resolution) ‚Äî so the proven writer just needed a trigger; authority boundary held (name/phone/email only). (4) **Shared `normalizePhone(raw)`** (`packages/shared/src/utils/normalizePhone.ts`, exported from the barrel + `@trace/shared/utils/normalizePhone`) ‚Äî the rule-of-three storage normalizer (trim ¬∑ collapse whitespace ¬∑ empty‚Üínull) now called by all three phone writes (R1 OwnerSignup, R3 Settings, Profile); distinct from the SMS E.164 normalizer (`send.ts`) and the live-input display formatter (`CustomerCapture.formatPhone`). NO schema/RLS/owner_id/full_name/login-email changes. **BUILDER-COMPLETE; owner-proof owed** (no onboarding phone field; owner `/profile` phone persists to `business_members.phone`; no duplicate `businesses` row creatable). Close-out ledger row #28.

**Onboarding address round-trip + leakage relabel ‚Äî 2026-06-25 (FIX 2 `2c7bf08` / FIX 3 `0a18ca1`):** (FIX 2) the wizard load effect SELECTed only `id,name`, so `businesses.address` never populated the field/review and the normal `finalize()` path never wrote a typed address back (only the legacy create branch did) ‚Üí a typed address was silently dropped. Now the load effect SELECTs `address` (both biz-from-url + fallback branches) and seeds `nurseryInfo.address`; `finalize()` writes it back via an owner-scoped `businesses.address` UPDATE on every path (idempotent on the legacy create). `[TRACE:ONBOARD]` on address load/save. (FIX 3) the slider-driven LeakagePath result, "Annual revenue left on the table," read like a finding about the user's real business ‚Äî relabeled "Estimated annual leakage at your volume" + weekly line reframed as a projection (wording only, no logic). NO schema/RLS changes. **BUILDER-COMPLETE; owner-proof owed** (typed onboarding address persists to `businesses.address`; leakage reads as an estimate). Close-out ledger rows #34/#35.

## Business Creation Abuse Guards (Shared)

**What:** Three opt-in guards that run at the `createBusinessAndMember()` chokepoint in `OwnerSignup.tsx` before any `businesses` row is inserted. All three ship **OFF by default** (`false`). OFF = clean base case, zero queries, zero effect. ON = fully enforces. No partial state.  
**Status:** ‚úÖ Built 2026-06-11 ‚Äî wired into OwnerSignup.tsx; all flags OFF  
**Vertical:** shared | **Type:** infrastructure  
**Location:** `packages/shared/src/auth/businessGuards.ts`  
**Entry point:** `runBusinessCreationGuards(userId, supabase)` ‚Äî runs A ‚Üí B ‚Üí C in order; first non-allowed result short-circuits; passes merge `insertPatch` to caller

**Guards:**

| Guard | Flag | Default | Behavior when ON |
|---|---|---|---|
| **GUARD_A** `PER_IDENTITY_FREE_TIER` | `GUARD_A_PER_IDENTITY_FREE_TIER` | `false` | Queries `businesses` for prior rows by this owner. If ‚â•1 prior business exists ‚Üí sets `insertPatch: { trial_started_at: null }` ‚Äî new business skips free trial. First business is unaffected. |
| **GUARD_B** `CREATION_RATE_LIMIT` | `GUARD_B_CREATION_RATE_LIMIT` | `false` | Queries `businesses` for rows created in last 24 h by this owner. If recentCount ‚â• 5 ‚Üí returns `{ allowed: false, error: '‚Ä¶' }` ‚Äî blocks creation with a user-visible message. |
| **GUARD_C** `SUSPICIOUS_PATTERN_REVIEW` | `GUARD_C_SUSPICIOUS_PATTERN_REVIEW` | `false` | Queries `businesses` for last-24h rows. If count ‚â• 10 AND all have `trial_started_at IS NOT NULL` ‚Üí returns `{ allowed: true, heldForReview: true }`. Creation proceeds but caller receives flag for admin surfacing. ‚öÝÔ∏è Requires `businesses.status` column before activating `insertPatch: { status: 'review_pending' }`. |

**Fail-open discipline:** Guard query errors return `{ allowed: true }` ‚Äî guard infrastructure failures never block a legitimate business creation.

**Activation discipline (documented in file, not yet activated):**
1. Prove base add-business flow with all three guards OFF (David + second business test, unimpeded).
2. Turn each guard ON one-at-a-time in isolation. David says "proven" ‚Üí leave ON.
3. GUARD_C prerequisite before activation: `ALTER TABLE businesses ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS status text DEFAULT 'active';` then uncomment `insertPatch` line in `checkGuardC()`.

**‚õî HARD LAUNCH GATE ‚Äî must be ON-and-tested before public self-serve business creation opens:**
While creation is private/invite-only (David + family), guards may stay OFF ‚Äî no abuse surface. When self-serve opens, all three guards must be individually activated, tested, and proven by David. This is a **launch prerequisite**, not a suggestion.

**`[TRACE:GUARD_A/B/C]` logs:** fire only when the respective flag is `true`. In default OFF state, zero logs emitted (clean base case per STD-003).

## Pain-Point Onboarding Wizard (Ignition OS ‚Äî NOW ACTIVATED via ?demo=)

**What:** Full 5-step demo-first onboarding wizard. Three pain-point scenarios show dollar value within 30 minutes ‚Äî no prior data entry required.  
**Status:** ‚úÖ ACTIVATED 2026-06-10 ‚Äî wired to `?demo=true` and `?demo=quick` URL params in CoreApp  
**Vertical:** ignition | **Type:** capability  
**Location:** `packages/ignition-os/OnboardingWizard.jsx` (root level)

**Steps (STEPS array):**
- `WELCOME` ‚Äî "Done leaving money on the table" + 3 pain-point teasers
- `SHOP_SETUP` ‚Äî shop name, owner name, 4-digit PIN (skipped in quickMode)
- `CHOOSE_PATH` ‚Äî scenario picker (3 choices)
- `PATH_EXPERIENCE` ‚Äî chosen scenario runs live
- `TEAM_QR` ‚Äî "Shop is live" ‚Äî QR code + role picker (Tech/Front Office) + invite link

**Three scenarios in PATH_EXPERIENCE:**
1. **MARGIN** (`MarginPath`) ‚Äî enter vendor cost + price charged ‚Üí `MarginEngine.calculateRetail()` ‚Üí suggested price + "margin leak detected" + annual $ via weekly-parts slider
2. **DIAGNOSE** (`DiagnosePath`) ‚Äî pick fault code from FAULT_LIBRARY (6 codes) or type own ‚Üí full estimate (parts + labor + margin) ‚Üí save as first work order
3. **MIGRATE** (`MigratePath`) ‚Äî import customers from QuickBooks / CSV / manual entry

**Launch URLs:**
- `?demo=true` ‚Äî full walkthrough from WELCOME (5 steps, owner enters real shop name + PIN)
- `?demo=quick` ‚Äî jump to CHOOSE_PATH; pre-filled with "Demo Shop" / PIN 1234 (zero typing required for fast demoing)

**finalize() behavior:** generates new shopId (UUID), seeds DataBridge (localStorage), upserts to Supabase `shops` table, saves owner PIN to `DataBridge.user_profiles`. After `onComplete()` ‚Üí CoreApp clears URL param + enters main app.

**Margin engine used:** `packages/ignition-os/MarginEngine.js` (FULL engine ‚Äî 4 slabs, tier discounts, analyzeTransaction). NOT the shared 17-line stub. Demo output is accurate.

**quickMode prop:** `<DemoWizard quickMode={true} />` ‚Äî skips WELCOME and SHOP_SETUP, initializes `stepIndex=2` (CHOOSE_PATH), pre-fills shopInfo/ownerName/ownerPin defaults.

## Customer Management (cap 3.7, Cultivar OS) ‚Äî OWNER-PROVEN 2026-07-03

**What:** The consolidated customer-management surface ‚Äî roster + edit + dedup + person/org identity. Four proven pieces:
- **Roster (#81, `52997c0`)** ‚Äî `/customers`, the 3rd `DataSheet<T>` consumer (after `/inventory` + `/assets`) ‚Äî the list David/Lauren expect + inline edit, owner-only. See "Customers Roster" below for the full detail.
- **In-context edit modal (#82, `3e7806a`)** ‚Äî a delivery card's "Edit customer" opens an owner-only `CustomerEditModal` OVER the current route/map (per-field-on-blur, no Save button) instead of navigating to `/customers`. Shares ONE form body (`CustomerFields`) + ONE rule set (`customerEdit.ts` ‚Äî `coerceCustomerField`/`persistCustomerField`) with the roster (no drift). Files: `CustomerEditModal.tsx`, `CustomerFields.tsx`, `customerEdit.ts`, `Customers.tsx`, `DeliverySchedule.tsx`.
- **Person/org classifier (#83, `74667bc`, `customer_type`)** ‚Äî OCR `customer_kind` classification ‚Üí a person splits first/last + links the people spine; an organization keeps its whole name in `first_name` (`last_name=''`), `customer_type='organization'`, and SKIPS the people spine. Migration `20260702_customers_customer_type.sql` (`customer_type text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'person'`, NO CHECK ‚Äî `price_tier` precedent, AC-4) applied by David; backfill approved. Files: `api/receipts/ocr.ts`, `ReceiptKeeper.tsx`, `customerUpsert.ts`.
- **Org-dedup (`b33786c`, ledger #84)** ‚Äî a repeat organization matches on `business_id` + normalized(name) + normalized(billing address) ‚Üí REUSE the existing customer id + ADD a delivery, never mint a duplicate, never match on ship-to. Proven BOTH directions: Cedar Park HOA (repeat SAME site ‚Üí one customer, deliveries multiply) + Dave's Tree Service (3 job-sites Leander/Georgetown/Dripping Springs ‚Üí one customer, three deliveries). File: `customerUpsert.ts`.

**Identity model:** customer identity lives on the `customers` row; delivery destination (ship-to) lives on the `deliveries` row ‚Üí fixing a customer's name once reflects on every delivery view.

**Board:** üìã cap **3.7** üü¢. **Contractor/tier pricing ‚Äî Layers 1+2 BUILT + GENERALIZED to a Discounts admin item (2026-07-10, owner-proof owed):** tier‚Üídiscount is a standalone admin surface **Discounts** at `/discounts` (`manage_settings`-gated; **relocated OUT of Cost-to-Produce Block 5** ‚Äî Block 5 removed, extracted-not-duplicated). Generalized to owner-named **discount TYPES √ó N tiers**, each tier a pricing **BASIS** ‚Äî `retail_minus_percent` (% off the stored sell_price, D-35) **or** `at_cost` (server-read `unit_cost`, margin 0; **graceful degradation** ‚Äî no cost on file ‚Üí NEUTRAL retail fallback, never $0, `pricingNotes` order note, D-9). Config rides `business_pricing_config.config.discountTypes` jsonb additively (legacy flat `pricingTiers` **forward-migrated non-destructively** on read). ONE shared arithmetic (`packages/shared/src/business-logic/tierPricing.ts`): kept `applyTierDiscount` (19 tests) + ADDED `normalizeDiscountTypes`/`resolveTier`/`applyTierPrice` (40/40 tests total). `submit.ts` resolves the customer's tier server-side, reads `unit_cost` server-side (cost NEVER from client ‚Äî money-safe), applies the basis; `[TRACE:PRICE]` logs basis+resolved. **READ/WRITE split (¬ßB):** WRITE = `manage_settings` (pricing authority); READ of the set stays business-scoped in the data layer (`readPricingConfig`+`normalizeDiscountTypes`) ‚Äî the relocation did NOT drag the read behind admin-only (roster picker + checkout resolve tiers independently of the route). `/customers` roster + Add-Customer pickers present the full type‚Üítier set dynamically. business_type-seeded suggestion palette (DATA, AC-1) + "+ Custom"; retail floor non-deletable; tier-name uniqueness + % 0‚Äì100 enforced (FIX 5); warn-before-remove via owner-RLS customers count (no endpoint). **AI_BI (¬ßD):** toggle-gated (`config.aiBiEnabled`, owner setting on Discounts, default OFF) PLACEHOLDER advisory card on the Customers surface ‚Äî reads nothing, changes nothing, never auto-assigns (D-38 advisory-only); `[TRACE:AI_BI]` on render; real spend‚Üítier inference is the post-demo AIEngine port. NEW shared `mergePricingConfig` (read-merge-write) so the 3 partial writers can't clobber the shared jsonb. ZERO migration, ZERO new api-fn (12/12), no auth change; verify exit 0 zero net-new; ledger row #110. `[TRACE:config]`/`[TRACE:PRICE]`/`[TRACE:AI_BI]` ON. **Layer 3 the contractor PROGRAM (register‚Üíverify‚Üíapprove‚Üínotify) is STORIED, NOT built** (`user_stories.md`; flow spec ¬ß3/¬ß4).

## Customers Roster (Cultivar OS)

**What:** The customer ROSTER + inline-edit surface ‚Äî the list David/Lauren expect (every customer created via OCR-invoice capture, QR checkout, or added by hand here) AND the edit surface, in one. The **3rd consumer of the shared `DataSheet<T>` engine** (after `/inventory` and `/assets`) ‚Äî config-only, mirrors `BusinessAssets.tsx` minus the `node_type` guard.
**Status:** ‚úÖ OWNER-PROVEN 2026-07-03 ‚Äî ledger #81 (committed `52997c0`)
**Vertical:** general (shared spine) | **Type:** tile + nav node
**Location:** `packages/cultivar-os/src/pages/Customers.tsx`
**Route:** `/customers` (private, **OWNER-ONLY** ‚Äî in the owner-only `PermissionRoute` group alongside `/costs`)

**Engine:** shared `components/datasheet/DataSheet.tsx` (`DataSheet<CustomerRow>` + `TextCell` + `sheetStyles`). No new shared code.

**Read/write:** owner-scoped `SELECT` on `customers` (`.eq('business_id', businessId)`, order by created_at desc). Inline-editable via per-field immediate RLS `UPDATE` (`.eq('id').eq('business_id')`, reload after each): first_name (never blank ‚Äî the identity), last_name (NOT NULL ‚Üí '' on clear), phone, email, address_line1, city, state, zip. Inline-editable tier (2026-07-09): `price_tier` is now an inline `SelectCell` of the configured tier names (writes `customers.price_tier`, business_id-scoped) ‚Äî drives the checkout tier discount; the Add-Customer sheet gained a tier picker (was omitted‚Üísilent retail). Display-only: source, qb_customer_id ("Synced"), created_at. person_id hidden. Add-Customer bottom sheet ‚Üí direct `insert` with `source='manual'`.

**Party record ‚Äî standard entity-completeness (2026-07-13, D-41 proposed ¬∑ ledger #118 ¬∑ migration `20260713_customers_party_record.sql` APPLIED + catalog-verified A-F by David 2026-07-13, UI owner-proof owed):** `customers` brought to the complete standard party record in ONE additive migration (15 cols): identity `organization_name`/`display_name`; **billing** `billing_line1/line2/city/state/zip` (**L1 ‚Äî billing on the customer; shipping is order-time, snapshotted on the `deliveries` row; `customer_addresses` saved ship-to book = deferred L2**); tax `tax_id`/`tax_exempt_expires`/`tax_exempt_cert_doc_url` (STD-010 ingest SLOT); terms `payment_terms`/`credit_limit`; lifecycle `status` (soft-deactivate) / `updated_at` (+ canonical `set_updated_at_generic()` trigger, STD-011) / `notes`. Existing unprefixed `address_*` LEFT UNTOUCHED. AC-1 (payment_terms/status string values, NO CHECK); RLS inherits (AC-3, no new policy); BENCH-C ‚Äî `tax_id`/`credit_limit` VALUE-MASKED in `[TRACE:customers]`. **UI shift:** the ~18-field set moved OFF the inline grid into a NEW grouped `CustomerPartyEditor` modal (`components/customers/CustomerPartyEditor.tsx` ‚Äî Identity ¬∑ Contact ¬∑ Billing ¬∑ Tax ¬∑ Commercial terms ¬∑ Status; auto-save via the shared coerce/persist helpers; the tax section reveals reason/cert/expiry and cannot save exempt without a reason ‚Äî mirrors D-40's server refusal, and this is what made the exemption UI-editable, closing the D-40 owner-prove blocker). The **roster is now LEAN** ‚Äî name (opens editor) ¬∑ type ¬∑ tier ¬∑ tax-exempt badge ¬∑ status (inline) ¬∑ Added ¬∑ Edit. Deploy-window-safe load (FULL‚ÜíCORE fallback on 42703/PGRST204). Home: `docs/decisions/2026-07-13-customer-party-record.md`. Follow-ups flagged: (a) org-name backfill out of first_name; (b) unprefixed address_* ‚Üí billing cleanup; (c) cert-doc ingest via STD-010; (d) L2 `customer_addresses` ship-to book.

**STD-011 UI unification ‚Äî ONE customer form (2026-07-13, ledger #119):** Add and Edit now render the SAME `CustomerPartyEditor` ‚Äî the old flat 8-field Add form (`CustomerFields` + a direct `handleSubmit` insert) is RETIRED. The editor gained a `mode: 'create' | 'edit'`: create starts empty, buffers all fields, and does ONE INSERT on "Save Customer" (shared `insertCustomer`, owner RLS, BENCH-C-masked); edit is per-field auto-save (unchanged). The ONLY differences are title / empty-vs-populated / insert-vs-update. Required-first_name + exempt-requires-reason validation apply in both modes. NO-regression bridge: the editor mirrors Billing ‚Üí the legacy consumed `address_*` on save (both modes), keeping checkout/delivery addresses populated until follow-up (b) repoints readers to `billing_*`. `CustomerEditModal` (delivery-card quick edit) remains the deliberate lightweight contextual subset. NO migration, NO new api-fn (12/12).

**Customer detail page `/customers/:id` with order history (2026-07-14, D-44 proposed ¬∑ ledger #122 ¬∑ BUILDER-COMPLETE, owner-proof owed):** the per-customer drill-in David asked for ("where do I view all of john smith's orders?") ‚Äî no such view existed (`/customers` was roster + edit modal only). New page `pages/CustomerDetail.tsx`: **header** (initials avatar ¬∑ name [org name if organization] ¬∑ type/tier/tax-exempt/status badges ¬∑ contact line ¬∑ "Edit record" button) ‚Üí **4 LIVE-computed stat cards** ‚Üí **order-history list** (rows link to the existing `/orders/:id`; line summary via `orderItemName`) ‚Üí **stubbed insights strip** (D-9 labeled marker "Insights ‚Äî coming ¬∑ spend trend, reorder cadence, margin"; NO fabricated numbers ‚Äî the post-demo AIEngine advisory hook). **Stats** computed live from this customer's own orders (`orders WHERE customer_id=:id AND business_id`, `created_at` desc ‚Äî `orders.customer_id` written by submit.ts:566): Orders = ALL (incl. cancelled); Lifetime value = Œ£ total EXCLUDING cancelled; Avg = lifetime √∑ non-cancelled count; Last = newest. **NO stored lifetime_value** (David's call ‚Äî one light indexed query). **Editing via the EXISTING `CustomerPartyEditor`** (STD-011 ‚Äî "Edit record" opens it in edit mode; the page does NOT re-implement the form). Roster **NAME click now navigates to the detail page** (`Customers.tsx`); the Edit button + tax badge still open the editor (roster quick-edit); tier/status inline unchanged. `select('*')` on the customer read = deploy-window-safe across the gated party/exemption cols. Owner-only route in the `/customers` `PermissionRoute` group (matches customers_business_owner + orders_business_owner owner-only RLS ‚Äî AC-3). BENCH-C: `[TRACE:customers]`/`[TRACE:ROSTER]` log ids/counts only (no PII; UUID URL). ZERO migration, ZERO new api-fn (12/12); verify exit 0 zero net-new; verify-universals cap #r EXCEPTIONS gains `/customers/:id` (same class as `/orders/:id`). Home: `docs/decisions/2026-07-14-customer-detail-page-order-history.md`.

**Gate (both layers agree):** tile `required_permission:'owner-only'` + route in the owner-only `PermissionRoute` group + standalone `nav_customers` NAV_IA node inheriting owner-only from the tile ‚Äî all matching the `customers_business_owner` RLS (owner-only, FOR ALL). A Staff session sees no tile, no nav entry, and is redirected from `/customers` ‚Üí nav never opens onto an empty RLS wall (Gate-3 lesson).

**v1 scope:** customers table ONLY. Person spine (`customers.person_id ‚Üí people`) deferred ‚Äî stays populated-on-create by the OCR/service-key path; the owner can't read other person rows anyway (people RLS is `people_self_all`, auth_user_id-keyed), so cross-role display ("also a vendor") is not possible here.

**Instrumentation:** `[TRACE:customers]` on load + every inline edit + insert (ON ‚Äî standing owner instruction).

**Owner-proof (David, 2026-07-03 ‚Äî PASSED):** `/customers` shows the roster (all OCR + hand-added customers); inline-edit a name/phone ‚Üí persists ‚Üí reflects on that customer's deliveries via the join; sort/search/hide-columns work; "Edit customer" from a delivery card now opens the in-context modal (#82); a Staff session cannot reach `/customers`.

## Campaign Scheduler (Cultivar OS)

**What:** Schedule, generate, and track social media campaigns. AI-generated post drafts with tone learning from copied posts. Owner copies text and posts manually ‚Äî no auto-publish.  
**Status:** ‚úÖ Built ‚Äî TypeScript (Cultivar OS only). advert_channels router live 2026-06-08. Blotato removed.  
**Vertical:** cultivar | **Type:** tile  
**Location:** `packages/cultivar-os/src/pages/Campaigns.tsx` + `CampaignDetail.tsx`  
**Route:** `/campaigns` + `/campaigns/:id` (private)

**Backend:**
- `packages/cultivar-os/api/campaigns.ts` ‚Äî combined action handler (action: 'generate' | 'copy-post'). **generate:** reads `business_modules.config.advert_channels`, generates ONLY for enabled channels, derives post count from campaign duration. No hardcoded channel names. **copy-post (handoff model):** copies text, marks status='published' (= owner reviewed, NOT auto-posted), saves edited pairs for tone learning.
- `packages/shared/src/campaigns/generate.ts` ‚Äî `generateCampaignPosts({ advertChannels, ... })`. `CHANNEL_GUIDANCE` map keyed by channel name. `postsPerChannel()` derives count from campaign days. `ADVERT_DEBUG` gated.

**Handoff controls (CampaignDetail.tsx):**
- [Edit] ‚Üí inline textarea ‚Üí save draft edits locally.
- [Copy caption] ‚Üí clipboard + calls copy-post action ‚Üí status='published'. SMS label: "Copy text".
- [‚Üì Image] ‚Üí stub, disabled (image generation seam).
- [Open ‚Üó] ‚Üí opens channel URL in new tab (social channels only; no Open for SMS).

**Schema:** `campaigns`, `campaign_posts`, `business_voice_samples` tables + RLS. Migration: `supabase/migrations/20260529_campaigns.sql` (original); `supabase/migrations/20260613_business_voice_samples.sql` (renamed + source column).
- `campaign_posts.platform` stores the channel name (from `advert_channels[].name`).
- `business_voice_samples`: `(business_id, platform, original_text, edited_text, source)` ‚Äî accumulates with every copy-post where owner edited. `source='campaign_generate'`. VERIFIED 2026-06-13 (C1‚ÄìC6 CLEAN). Proof: `docs/verification/20260613_business_voice_samples_verification.md`.

**Dashboard integration:** "Campaign Scheduler" card shows green border when drafts are pending.

**Hidden seams declared (inert ‚Äî see `api/campaigns.ts` SEAM DECLARATIONS):**
- `auto-publish seam` ‚Äî wire adapter here when activated. Gate: demand + pricing.
- `sms-auto-send seam` ‚Äî TCPA/consent compliance at activation; adopt provider model. Gate: demand + pricing + provider.

**‚öÝÔ∏è David must apply migration:** `supabase/migrations/20260608_advert_channels_config.sql` migrates existing `{ platforms, cadence }` config to `{ advert_channels, cadence }`. Run VERIFICATION query in migration file after applying.

## Discovery Module (Cultivar OS ‚Äî v0)

**What:** Silent partner analysis engine. Fetches a prospect's website, runs a two-pass AI analysis (fast identity extraction + deep profile), and generates a "silent partner" email: what the business is doing well, what could amplify it. David sends the analysis to the prospect; they receive something real and specific regardless of whether they ever sign up.  
**Status:** ‚úÖ v0 built ‚Äî TypeScript (2026-06-05). See DISCOVERY_MODULE_BRIEF.md for full spec.  
**Vertical:** cultivar (admin surface today; cross-vertical engine) | **Type:** capability  
**Location:** `packages/shared/src/discovery/` + `packages/cultivar-os/api/discovery/ingest.ts` + `packages/cultivar-os/src/pages/DiscoveryInspect.tsx`

**v0 flow (fully operational):**
1. David opens `/discovery/inspect` (internal, URL is the gate ‚Äî no auth wall)
2. Enters prospect URL, vertical, optional pain point
3. Engine runs: website fetch ‚Üí Haiku identity pass ‚Üí Sonnet deep analysis ‚Üí Sonnet synthesis email
4. David reviews profile + draft email in DiscoveryInspect
5. Enters prospect email ‚Üí clicks "Send analysis" ‚Üí Resend delivers the silent partner email

**Engine:**
- `discovery/adapters/website.ts` ‚Äî fetches URL, extracts text (Chrome headers, fallbacks to /about)
- `discovery/engine.ts` ‚Äî `runIdentity()` (Haiku, fast), `runAnalysis()` (Sonnet, deep); routes through `packages/shared/src/ai/execute.ts`
- `discovery/synthesis.ts` ‚Äî `runSynthesis()`: BusinessDiscoveryProfile ‚Üí SilentPartnerAnalysis; routes through `execute.ts`
- `discovery/seed.ts` ‚Äî `seedServiceOfferings()`: maps suggestedOfferings ‚Üí `service_offerings` rows with `is_active=false`; idempotent

**API (cultivar-os):**
- `api/discovery/ingest.ts` ‚Äî POST `/api/discovery/ingest`
  - Default: fetch ‚Üí identity ‚Üí analysis ‚Üí synthesis ‚Üí `{ identity, profile, analysis, seeded }`
  - `businessId` in body ‚Üí seeds service_offerings in-memory immediately after analysis (no DB lookup)
  - `action='send'` in body ‚Üí delivers analysis email via notifications module (no new Vercel function)

**Admin surface:**
- `pages/DiscoveryInspect.tsx` ‚Äî form (URL + vertical + pain point) ‚Üí loading stages ‚Üí profile display ‚Üí analysis preview ‚Üí Copy button + Send section (recipient email input + "Send analysis" button)

**Notification template:**
- `notifications/templates/cultivar.ts` ‚Üí `silent_partner_analysis` ‚Äî transactional email, TRACE default branding (not LAWNS). Pre-rendered HTML from synthesis passes through.

**‚öÝÔ∏è Env vars required for live email delivery (not yet set in Vercel):** `RESEND_API_KEY` + `FROM_EMAIL`. Without them, `sendNotification` runs in demo mode: logs the send, returns `{ ok: true, demo: true }` ‚Äî no actual email delivery.

**remaining:**
- Discovery persistence ‚Äî NOT built. `seed.ts` wired in-memory via `ingest.ts`; v0 admin sends analysis live with no retained copy. DB persistence (`discovery_sessions`, `business_discovery_profiles`), seed-at-signup via lookup, and retained session copies = v2 (gated surface + one-auth). GAP not debt. Horizon: v2/later.

### Discrepancy-Compare ‚Äî entered data vs LIVE site (capability 1.1) ‚Äî added 2026-06-19

**What:** During onboarding, compares the business data an owner ENTERED against what their OWN live website actually says, and surfaces honest, **hedged** discrepancies ("Your site shows X for your phone, but you entered Y ‚Äî should we update it?"). Closes the gap between stale entered data and the public site without ever asserting a correction.
**Status:** ‚úÖ BUILDER-COMPLETE (2026-06-19); owner-proof = run against a real entered-vs-site mismatch. **Type:** capability | **Vertical:** cross-vertical (shared).
**Location:** `packages/shared/src/discovery/compare.ts` (+ `compare.test.ts`, 17/17), exported from `discovery/index.ts`; AI capability `discovery_compare` in `ai/capabilities.ts`.
- `compareEnteredVsSite(entered, {apiKey})` ‚Äî interrogates the **LIVE** site via `fetchWebsiteContent` (no cache/history; `fetchedAt` carried through proves freshness), extracts site values through the AI gateway, returns D-9-gated discrepancies.
- **Honesty (D-9), three gates in `filterDiscrepancies`:** (1) site must state a value; (2) entered vs site must genuinely differ (`looksSame` ignores case/punctuation/spacing); (3) confidence must clear threshold (default drops `low`). The owner-facing message is built by `buildDiscrepancyMessage` ‚Äî always a QUESTION, never declares which value is correct (hedge = code guarantee, not model prose). Unreachable site ‚Üí zero fabricated discrepancies, AI not even called.
- Emits `[TRACE:DISCOVERY]` (compare:start / compare:unreachable / compare:done) ON by default.

### Sandbox Seeder ‚Äî branded 7-day sample data (capability 1.2, onboarding Phase 2) ‚Äî added 2026-06-19

**What:** Makes a brand-new vertical's dashboard ALIVE on arrival instead of empty ‚Äî seeds a believable, BRANDED 7-day slice of sample sales/activity under the business's own name. Every row is labelled sample/sandbox so it is unmistakable and EXACTLY removable; the label "comes off" when real data loads (`clear()`). Also the reusable `clear()` the Wave-2 real-populate will call.
**Status:** ‚úÖ BUILDER-COMPLETE (2026-06-19) ‚Äî `--verify` proves seed‚Üícount‚Üíclear leaves exactly zero sandbox rows and real data untouched (run against demo tenant: 6 customers / 5 plants / 5 inventory lots / 12 orders incl. 2 leakage, branded "LAWNS Tree Farm LLC"). **Type:** tool/script | **Vertical:** cultivar (tenant-agnostic by `business_id`).
**Location:** `scripts/seed-sandbox.mjs` ‚Äî `seed()` / `clear()` for one `business_id`.
- Markers (clear deletes ONLY these, never real rows): `customers.source='sandbox'`, `cultivar_plants.tag_id LIKE 'SMPL-%'`, `business_inventory.sku LIKE 'SMPL-%'`, `orders.notes LIKE '[SANDBOX]%'`.
- Seeds: customers, cultivar_plants (identity), business_inventory (lots ‚Äî also lights up the empty-5.1 inventory surface), orders spread over the last 7 days (varied totals, 2 leakage flags) ‚Üí Dashboard today-revenue / week-orders / leakage tiles all populate.
- Emits `[TRACE:SEED]` (seed/clear with counts) ON by default.
- Usage: `node scripts/seed-sandbox.mjs --business=<uuid>` (clear+seed), `--clear`, `--verify`.

### Catalog-Populate ‚Äî read live site ‚Üí write their REAL catalog (capability 1.3, the onboarding wow) ‚Äî added 2026-06-21

**What:** Reads a nursery's LIVE website, extracts their REAL catalog (varieties + category, per-item extraction confidence), CLEARS the sandbox sample data, and writes their actual varieties into `business_inventory` ‚Äî so a new dashboard shows THEIR trees, not generic samples. The existing discovery engine extracts services/identity only; this is the missing CATALOG cut.
**Status:** ‚úÖ BUILDER-COMPLETE (2026-06-21) ‚Äî proven live against **lawnstrees.com**: 30 pages crawled ‚Üí **114 real varieties** extracted (Oak, Crape Myrtle, Cypress, Redbud, Vitex ‚Ä¶) ‚Üí written to `business_inventory`, idempotent (clear‚Üípopulate‚Üíclear leaves 0 orphans), real LAWNS rows untouched. **OWNER-PROOF owed** (David: run on his LAWNS tenant with the Vercel ANTHROPIC key, watch the catalog materialize on `/inventory`, then clear). **Type:** capability | **Vertical:** cross-vertical (shared), proven on cultivar.
**Location:** `packages/shared/src/discovery/catalog.ts` (crawler + AI extractor + D-9 mapping) + `discovery/populate.ts` (orchestration) + `catalog.test.ts` (35/35 adversarial), exported from `discovery/index.ts`; AI capability `discovery_catalog` (Haiku) in `ai/capabilities.ts`; runner `scripts/populate-catalog.ts`; gated table `business_discovery_profiles` (migration `20260621`, gate `scripts/verify-discovery-profiles.mjs`).
- **Crawl:** `fetchCatalogPages` does a bounded 2-level crawl (entry ‚Üí hub pages like `/shop/` ‚Üí category pages), reuses `fetchWebsiteContent` per page; generic link heuristics (WooCommerce `/product-category/` + hand-rolled patterns); degrades to the entry page when no catalog links exist.
- **Extract:** `extractCatalog` runs the `discovery_catalog` model per batched page ‚Üí `{variety, botanical, category, confidence}`; dedups by variety (keeps highest confidence; tie-breaks prefer a SPECIFIC category over a catch-all like "All Trees", and an item carrying a botanical name).
- **Honesty (D-9 ‚Äî the whole contract):** low-confidence OR no-clear-category items are **FLAGGED** (`status='review'`, reason in `notes`), never silently coerced; **price is UNKNOWN** (`unit_cost=null`, `cost_confidence='UNKNOWN'`) ‚Äî never 0 (the site has no prices); **qty=0** (never fabricated); **`cultivar_plants` deliberately NOT populated** (per-specimen/QR identity doesn't exist on a bare-domain QR ‚Äî writing it would be fabrication). The dashboard's `status` + `cost_confidence` badges visibly separate "sure" from "verify me".
- **Idempotent markers:** `business_inventory.sku LIKE 'DISC-%'` / `notes LIKE '[DISCOVERY]%'`. Populate clears BOTH the 1.2 sandbox (`SMPL-`/`[SANDBOX]`, reusing `clearSandbox`) and prior discovery rows before writing.
- **`business_discovery_profiles`** (gated migration) stores the full `raw_extract` (items + confidences + counts) as the honesty/audit trail ‚Äî upsert on `(business_id, source_url)`.
- Emits `[TRACE:POPULATE]` (crawl / extract / clear / populate) ON by default.
- **Size-variant parser real-page PROOF (2026-06-30, verification artifact ‚Äî NOT a capability change):** `extractSizeVariants` (the deterministic, no-AI WooCommerce size parser, ledger #62) is now proven against the **real** LAWNS Vitex page, not just synthetic fixtures. Pinned offline fixture `packages/shared/src/discovery/__fixtures__/lawns-vitex-real.html` (real `https://lawnstrees.com/product/shoal-creek-vitex/`, fetched 2026-06-30, **sanitized**: Mailchimp API key + connected-site ids + GA/GTM ids + business phone redacted ‚Äî size markup `data-product_variations`/`<select>` preserved byte-for-byte) + proof script `scripts/prove-vitex-variants.ts` (default OFFLINE/deterministic; `--live` flag for a network re-fetch). Asserts the **JSON-primary** path yields exactly `["5 Gallon","15 Gallon","30 Gallon","45 Gallon"]` in order, no invented sizes / no enum coercion, and the dry-run rows populate WOULD write (one per Vitex √ó size, `variant_group=parent slug`, honesty contract qty 0 / cost UNKNOWN) ‚Äî **10/10**, DRY-RUN only (nothing written to any catalog). Does NOT change capability state: live populate-into-real-catalog + the count-side picker owner-prove on populated data remain OWED/gated.
- **Dup-size data-quality surfacing at WRITE time (2026-06-30, ledger #74, BUILDER-COMPLETE, app-code-only):** populate now DETECTS a `(variant_group, size)` collision before insert and SURFACES it, closing the silent dead-end the stress battery (#73 recon) found ‚Äî two rows sharing one `variant_group` + the same `size` made a variety silently uncountable-by-scan at count time (`detectSizeCollision`'s all-distinct check fails ‚Üí UNKNOWN, indistinguishable from never-seen). **Refuse-to-guess is UNCHANGED** (`detectSizeCollision` untouched; we detect + surface, never dedupe/auto-pick ‚Äî both rows still written). New pure exported `findDuplicateSizeGroups(rows)` in `populate.ts` runs after row-expansion ‚Üí emits `[TRACE:POPULATE] data-quality:dup-size` + adds `PopulateResult.dataQuality.dupSizeGroups` + `raw_extract.counts.dupSizeGroups` (audit trail) + the `api/discovery/ingest.ts` `action=populate` response, so the owner sees it in the populate report before it reaches a count. Why populate is the right place: it's the importer, and `extractSizeVariants` already dedupes within one product, so the realistic dup is two varieties bound to one `sourceSlug`. `populate.test.ts` **9/9** (clean distinct sizes ‚Üí no finding; same group+same size ‚Üí flagged count 2; two varieties one slug ‚Üí flagged; null/parent rows never flagged; case-insensitive size match; cross-group same size NOT flagged). `npm run verify` exit 0 zero NET-NEW. Deferred (David's call): **B** count-time UNKNOWN distinction in `InventoryCount.tsx`; **C** DB unique constraint on `(business_id, variant_group, size)` (migration). No schema, no migration.

### Cost-Discovery ‚Äî cost-to-produce reasoning (Opus) ‚Üí `business_inventory` cost + confidence ‚Äî added 2026-06-21

**What:** A discovery capability that drives a short question flow REASONING about a grower's cost-to-produce for ONE inventory line (e.g. the LAWNS 30-gal Live Oak) and writes `business_inventory.unit_cost` + `cost_confidence`. Each owner answer re-runs the reasoning, so confidence SHARPENS as inputs accumulate ‚Äî typically ESTIMATED (a stated guess) ‚Üí DERIVED (computed from confirmed inputs). Routed to **Opus** (reasoning-under-uncertainty) via the existing per-capability model routing, with the per-business `business_modules.config` override still honored. Mirrors the catalog-discovery honesty posture, pointed at COST instead of variety. NOT a schema change ‚Äî `unit_cost` (nullable) + `cost_confidence` (CONFIRMED|DERIVED|ESTIMATED|UNKNOWN) already exist (`20260612_business_assets_inventory_cost_confidence.sql`).
**Status:** ‚úÖ BUILDER-COMPLETE (2026-06-21) ‚Äî `costDiscovery.test.ts` **26/26** adversarial (no live AI) + `scripts/verify-cost-discovery.ts` **9/9** against LIVE `business_inventory` on the service key (ESTIMATED written ‚Üí SHARPENS to DERIVED ‚Üí forced-CONFIRMED **BLOCKED**, row unchanged ‚Üí UNKNOWN leaves the line as-is ‚Üí cleanup). **OWNER-PROOF owed** (David: run a cost-discovery pass through real UI under real RLS on a real line, watch confidence move ESTIMATED‚ÜíDERIVED as he answers, and see it refuse to claim CONFIRMED without a receipt ‚Äî needs a small UI panel on `/inventory` as the surface). **Type:** capability | **Vertical:** cross-vertical (shared), proven on cultivar.
**Location:** `packages/shared/src/discovery/costDiscovery.ts` (engine: prompt + code honesty-guard + turn driver + writer) + `costDiscovery.test.ts` (26/26), exported from `discovery/index.ts`; AI capability `discovery_cost` (**Opus `claude-opus-4-8`**) in `ai/capabilities.ts`; wired into the existing `api/discovery/ingest.ts` as `action='cost-discovery'` (one turn) + `action='cost-apply'` (write) ‚Äî **no new Vercel function** (12-fn ceiling, tech-debt #41); proof `scripts/verify-cost-discovery.ts`.
- **Honesty contract (enforced in CODE, not just the prompt ‚Äî the real risk surface):**
  - **NEVER CONFIRMED:** `guardReasoning` RAISES `CostConfidenceViolation` on any model attempt to claim CONFIRMED (reserved for receipt-linked cost, D-9 count-once seam); the writer re-rejects it at the DB boundary. Proven: a forced-CONFIRMED model output is blocked and the row is left untouched.
  - **NEVER fabricate:** a missing / non-numeric / zero / negative cost collapses to UNKNOWN (null) ‚Äî unknown stays UNKNOWN, never written as $0.
  - **ESTIMATED vs DERIVED:** ESTIMATED = owner's stated guess; DERIVED = computed from confirmed inputs and carries the `derivation` arithmetic. A DERIVED claim with no shown arithmetic is DEMOTED to ESTIMATED ‚Äî a guess is never dressed up as a derivation.
  - **Declined leaves it where it was:** `applyCostReasoning` makes NO write on an UNKNOWN turn ‚Äî the line is left exactly as it was, honestly labeled (never clobbered, never fabricated).
- **Tenant-safe write:** updates `business_inventory` scoped by `(id, business_id)` ‚Äî never cross-tenant.
- Emits `[TRACE:COSTDISC]` (turn / guard / apply) ON by default per the standing owner instruction.

### Design Record ‚Äî Grower Import, Margin Referee, Role√óDevice Visibility (DOC ONLY) ‚Äî added 2026-06-21

**What:** Durable capture of the 2026-06-21 grower-scan design session ‚Äî NOT a build. Records the experiment result (28 growers / 1378 items / 0 fabrication; import BLOCKED on a cost-ledger schema with no home for sell price, price basis, or size) and the locked design for: grower import, the **margin referee** (cost + sell price + floor, fires only at CONFIRMED/DERIVED, verdict always carries confidence), **role√ódevice visibility** (ROLE = security ceiling enforced at the DATA layer √ó CONTEXT/DEVICE = owner-tunable focus ‚Äî one additive mobile-flag column on Ignition's role‚Üífield config), AI routing by kind of cognition (OCR=cheap extraction / cost discovery=Opus reasoning), the onboarding honesty gradient, and the CSV-at-OCR-door rule.
**Status:** ‚úÖ Doc written. Design LOCKED; **schema gap unbuilt** (needs additive nullable `sell_price` + `price_basis` PAIR + `size_or_container` ‚Äî D-9 UNKNOWN-never-zero, overlaps tech-debt #42 residual). **Type:** decision record | **Vertical:** cross-vertical.
