### Decision Record ‚Äî Role-Based Financial Permissions v1 (DOC ONLY) ‚Äî added 2026-06-21

**What:** Sign-off artifact for the role-permission hardening build that follows ‚Äî NOT a build. Records the verified problem (role enforcement is RENDER-ONLY: `business_members.permissions` JSONB read into context but consulted by no RLS policy or API; exactly one render gate fires; ~26 sensitive columns across 6 tables sit owner_all+member_all only; tenant isolation AC-2/AC-3 intact and SEPARATE). Decides the **four permissions** (view_wages, view_pricing_config, view_costs, view_margin ‚Äî view_margin requires view_costs), **role defaults** (Owner=all four; Manager=costs+margin not pricing-config/wages; Tech=none), and the **hybrid enforcement by data class** (HARD data-layer wall via RLS + column masking for wages + pricing_config; ROLE-AWARE RESPONSE SHAPING for costs + margin because the server consumes unit_cost in checkout #11/#12 + dashboard rollups and a flat RLS-deny would NULL totals across 14 multi-role SELECT sites; render gates are the top convenience layer only). Binding doctrine: DEFAULT-DENY ¬∑ SINGLE CHOKEPOINT (can()/checkPermission()) ¬∑ RESTRICTIVE-FIRST/EXPAND-ONLY ¬∑ PROOF BAR (low-role direct query refused at network response, not render-absence).
**Status:** ‚úÖ Doc written. Decision LOCKED; **enforcement unbuilt** (build owes: mint+seed four permissions + backfill current owners before flipping on ¬∑ wire dormant chokepoint ¬∑ column-masking approach chosen at build ¬∑ per-site hand-verify the 14 SELECT sites ¬∑ resolve checkout public-path unit_cost shaping). Two-bar / RLS gates N/A this pass; the build owes both bars. **Type:** decision record | **Vertical:** cross-vertical.
**Location:** [docs/decisions/2026-06-21-role-financial-permissions.md](decisions/2026-06-21-role-financial-permissions.md). Source recon: `data/grower-scan/role-enforcement-ground-truth.md`.

### Standard ‚Äî STD-011 ONE CANONICAL REPRESENTATION PER FACT (DOC ONLY) ‚Äî added 2026-06-22

**What:** New numbered standard in STANDARDS.md ‚Äî NOT a build. A single-meaning fact (access/state booleans, tenant predicates, enum/status value sets, driftable config values) MUST have exactly ONE canonical representation referenced everywhere, never re-derived or duplicated; two representations of one fact can silently disagree, and in access/boundary/value facts that silence IS the leak. Encodes: state‚Üíone column via one shared helper (e.g. SECURITY DEFINER `is_active_member()`, which also resolves RLS recursion); enum‚Üíone allowed-value definition; config‚Üíone home per the config doctrine. Enforcement: a new sensitive column/policy re-deriving a fact = INCOMPLETE; a consistency sweep is a recognized correctness-hardening tool. Promotes AC-4 to a data-integrity invariant with a security consequence.
**Status:** ‚úÖ Standard written into STANDARDS.md (¬ßSTD-011 + ENFORCEMENT row + CHANGELOG v1.9). **Type:** standard | **Vertical:** cross-vertical.
**Origin:** the membership-active RLS consistency sweep ‚Äî `data/grower-scan/member-rls-consistency-audit.md` (3 spellings of "active member"; `md_self` omitted the active filter ‚Üí revoked member kept self-device access). **Recorded open item:** owner-only operational tables (orders/customers/plants/order_items + pre-2026-06 tables) have NO member policy ‚Üí Staff RLS-blocked despite `view_orders`/`qr_checkout`; next hardening item is a PRODUCT decision (what does Staff see, scoped how, PII?). Cross-pointer in tech-debt only.
**Cross-refs:** [STANDARDS.md](../STANDARDS.md) ¬ßSTD-011 ¬∑ AC-4 / AC-2 / AC-3 ¬∑ config doctrine.

---

### Financial Permission Wall ‚Äî data-layer enforcement (RLS primitives + child-table splits) ‚Äî updated 2026-06-22

**What:** The data-layer enforcement of the role-financial-permissions decision (above). Two SECURITY DEFINER primitives + per-table RLS so a low-role member's cost/wage/pricing read is refused at the DATA layer (network response), not just hidden at render.
- **Primitives (canonical, owned by postgres, `search_path=''`, EXECUTE‚Üíauthenticated):** `is_active_member(business_id)` (membership truth ‚Äî `20260622_is_active_member_canonical_rls.sql`) + `has_permission(business_id, perm)` (active membership AND `permissions ? perm`, jsonb array-of-strings ‚Äî `20260622_oauth_secrets_relocation_and_cost_wall.sql`). Policies compose them: `is_active_member(X) AND has_permission(X,'view_costs')` (membership-then-permission, composed not fused).
- **HARD-WALL child-table splits (`20260621_financial_wall_phase2.sql`):** `labor_resource_wages` (HR pay, gated `view_wages`) + `business_pricing_config` (pricing recipe, gated `view_pricing_config`) ‚Äî sensitive values moved off the member-readable parent into role-gated child rows; member policies decomposed onto the two primitives 2026-06-22.
- **view_costs table gates (2026-06-22):** 6 cost tables (`cost_objects`, `business_inventory`, `cost_object_edges`, `cost_object_assignments`, `business_service_log`, `receipts`) + `labor_resources` (view_wages) ‚Äî member policy = `is_active_member AND has_permission`. (The view_costs data gate was NEVER built before this ‚Äî cost tables had been membership-only; recon `data/grower-scan/cost-wall-leak-scope.md`.)
- **Render layer (top convenience tier only, NOT the boundary):** `PermissionRoute permission={VIEW_COSTS}` wraps `/costs /inventory /assets /operating-costs /pmi` (`packages/cultivar-os/src/router.tsx`); chokepoint `can()`/`has_permission()` in `BusinessProvider`. Permission constants: `packages/shared/src/auth/financialPermissions.ts`.

**Status:** ‚úÖ READ-WALL OWNER-PROVEN (Staff HAR: cost reads return 200 [], RLS row-filter; tamper 3/0; migrations live). ‚úÖ WRITE-WALL ‚Äî data-layer ENFORCED + the one bypass CLOSED (Gate-3b, 2026-06-22): the cost/wage member policies are `FOR ALL` with `has_permission` in `USING`+`WITH CHECK` (`20260622_‚Ä¶cost_wall.sql:141-212`) ‚Üí anon-key INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE refused for a member lacking the permission (recon-confirmed; write-tamper proof `scripts/verify-write-wall.ts`). The lone service-key bypass (costDiscovery `cost-apply`) is now caller-permission-gated (`api/discovery/ingest.ts` requires `view_costs` resolved from the auth context). Residual: render-layer button gates (operating-cost "+cost" shown to staff though the write is RLS-refused) = defense-in-depth, tech-debt #46.2. Enforces the D-009 moat on reads AND writes. Staff HAR detail: `trace_staff_only`, `isOwner:false`, `effectivePermissions` Array(3), no `view_costs`; every cost read (`cost_objects`, `business_inventory‚Ä¶unit_cost`, `business_pricing_config`) returned `200 []`. Artifact: `cultivar-os_vercel_app.har`. **Type:** capability (RLS/security) | **Vertical:** shared.

**Phase 3 Part A (render layer)** ‚Äî ‚è≥ BUILDER-COMPLETE, OWNER-PROVEN OWED-AFTER-DEPLOY. Code committed (`8918fe8`): `router.tsx:82` wraps `/costs|/inventory|/assets|/operating-costs|/pmi` in `<PermissionRoute permission={VIEW_COSTS}>`; `Dashboard.tsx:145` shapes the query (`.select(canViewCosts ? 'qty, unit_cost' : 'qty')`). In local `dist`; LIVE Vercel deploy + fresh Staff HAR owed: expect cost requests absent from the dashboard, the dashboard inventory query qty-only, and direct nav to gated routes redirects. (Part C grower-import ‚Äî checkout cost-as-price is the 2nd symptom of the `sell_price`/`price_basis` gap ‚Üí `docs/decisions/2026-06-21-grower-import-and-mobile-roles.md` + `data/grower-scan/inventory-fit-map.md`.)
**Cross-refs:** recon `data/grower-scan/cost-wall-leak-scope.md` ¬∑ decision `docs/decisions/2026-06-21-role-financial-permissions.md` ¬∑ STD-011.

### QB OAuth Secret Storage ‚Äî owner-only `business_accounting_secrets` ‚Äî added 2026-06-22

**What:** QuickBooks bearer secrets (`accounting_token` + `accounting_refresh_token`) relocated out of the member-readable `businesses` row into an owner-only table (Gate-3 credential leak: `businesses_member_select` exposed live QB tokens to active members). `business_accounting_secrets` (PK business_id FK‚Üíbusinesses CASCADE; `bas_owner_all` owner-only RLS, NO member policy). Realm ID + expiry + reconnect-flag + provider stay on `businesses` (non-secret, client-read). Shared accessor `packages/shared/src/quickbooks/secrets.ts` (`readQBSecrets`/`writeQBSecrets`, secrets-table-first + businesses-column fallback for deploy-window safety); repointed `quickbooks/refresh.ts`, `api/qbo/router.ts`, `api/qbo/invoice/cultivar.ts`. Migration: `20260622_oauth_secrets_relocation_and_cost_wall.sql` Part 1.

**Status:** ‚úÖ APPLIED (as postgres) ‚Äî `business_accounting_secrets` owner-only (`bas_owner_all`, no member policy); bearer tokens out of member reach. QB reconnect repointed to `writeQBSecrets`/`readQBSecrets` (`router.ts:133`, `refresh.ts:59`, `router.ts:182`, `invoice/cultivar.ts:112`); no bearer-token writes to `businesses` except `secrets.ts` deploy-window fallback. No regression. (Businesses columns NULLed; DROP = gated follow-up ‚Äî see tech-debt log.) **Type:** infrastructure (security) | **Vertical:** shared. **Header:** `secrets.ts` carries PURPOSE/DEPENDENCIES/OUTPUTS.

## Ignition OS ‚Äî Workflow Modules (2026-06-09 Reality Audit)

**Audit date:** 2026-06-09 | **Standard:** STD-010 (opaque name = debt; discovered build = catalogue it) | **Scope:** all .jsx/.js in `packages/ignition-os/` (root + modules/ + hooks/) | **Full report:** `docs/audits/ignition-reality-audit-2026-06-09.md`

> **Root-cause notes before the table:**
> - **DARK root cause:** `VITE_API_URL` not set in ignition-os Vercel project ‚Üí every `AIEngine.call()` returns `{ ok: false }`. Railway running but receives zero Vercel traffic.
> - **BROKEN root cause:** `20260602_ignition_drop_team_tables.sql` dropped `pin_resets`, `shop_invites`, `member_devices`. Only `shop_members` was recreated (`20260603_recreate_shop_members.sql`). The other three tables have no recreate migration.
> - **SPLIT-BRAIN root cause:** `IgnitionIntake` writes customers to Supabase `customers`. `IgnitionCRM` reads from DataBridge `customers_directory`. These are entirely separate stores ‚Äî intake customers never appear in CRM.

**Authoritative detail:** [`docs/audits/ignition-reality-audit-2026-06-09.md`](audits/ignition-reality-audit-2026-06-09.md) ‚Äî full module table, workflow chain, RBAC, and DataBridge orphaned keys.

> ‚öÝÔ∏è DEPRECATED ‚Äî the module table, workflow chain, RBAC section, and DataBridge orphaned keys below are bulk copies from the audit doc above. Remove in a later cleanup pass; read the audit doc for authoritative detail.

### Workflow Chain Summary

The RO chain is **mostly operational** end-to-end. Key degradation points:

```
Step 1 (Intake) ‚Üí ‚úÖ Step 2 (Queue) ‚Üí ‚úÖ Step 3 (Eval) ‚Üí ‚öÝÔ∏è DTC decode (3 codes only, rest DARK)
‚Üí Step 4 (Estimate: manual works, AI skeleton DARK, auto-PO DARK)
‚Üí Step 5 (Pricing: PORT path DataBridge, Estimate path Supabase ‚Äî NOT SYNCHRONIZED)
‚Üí Step 6 (Customer Auth: ‚úÖ digital signature)
‚Üí Step 7 (Kiosk: ‚úÖ labor/repair/custody)
‚Üí Step 8 (Invoice: ‚úÖ Supabase; PDF = stub; QB = DARK + no Vercel functions)
```

**QB note:** Cultivar OS has `api/qbo/*` Vercel functions. Ignition OS has NONE. QB is not just DARK ‚Äî the server-side functions do not exist for Ignition.

**Two parallel estimate paths (incompatible):** `IgnitionEstimate.jsx` (Supabase `estimates/estimate_line_items`) and `IgnitionPort.jsx` (DataBridge `active_job_context`). The same workflow step has two separate, unsynchronized data stores. Customer authorization via `CustomerApprovalPortal` works from both but writes to `customer_authorizations` (Supabase) in both cases.

### RBAC ‚Äî 19 Permissions, 4 Role Presets, Client-Side Only

Defined in `IgnitionAdmin.jsx ALL_PERMISSIONS`. Enforced by `CoreApp AccessGatekeeper` which checks DataBridge `current_user.permissions`. No Supabase RLS enforcement. Notable gap: `IgnitionCompliance.jsx` has `requiredPermissions={[]}` in CoreApp routing ‚Äî any logged-in user (including CUSTOMER role) can access the DOT inspection form.

### DataBridge Orphaned Keys

| Type | Key | Problem |
|---|---|---|
| Orphaned write | `margin_change_log` | Written by `DataBridge.setMarginConfig()`. No module reads or displays it. |
| Orphaned write | `pending_users` | Written by IgnitionOmni legacy staff enrollment. Only `EnrollmentCatch` reads it ‚Äî via an orphaned flow. |
| Orphaned read | `inventory_items` | IgnitionOmni reads for stats. IgnitionStok reads from Supabase `inventory` ‚Äî not DataBridge. Inventory value tile = always $0. |
| Orphaned read | `fleet_units` | IgnitionHub reads. No module in web build writes real fleet unit data. Hub shows empty GPS grid. |
| Orphaned read | `labor_guide` | `DataBridge.getLaborGuide()` always returns hardcoded defaults ‚Äî no module has ever written a real labor guide. |
